12:35 am May 12th, 2011














 lizzyling LJShare.link({"url":"http://lizzyling.livejournal.com/674.html","title":"Lizzy Ling dans la presse"});










Lizzy Ling dans la presse







Contact promo : flavie.rodriguez@gmail.comLIZZY LING fait partie de la compil Nouveaux talents Fnac – Believe Digital automne 2010En 2008 l’album UN TIGRE DANS LE BUNGALOW a reçu le soutien de la SACEM En 2010 l’album NO SIMILI a reçu le soutien de la SACEM et de l’ADAMIEN 2011 le clip Je Suis Pire (extrait de No simili) a reçu le soutien du FCM/CNC et de la SPPFLargement Playlisté dans tout le réseau Radio Quotas Playlists sur plusieurs ferarocks, campus, réseau francodiff et yacast.Lizzy est aussi la nouvelle voix féminine du groupe MY CONCUBINE album UNE CHAISE POUR TED (Happy home records / MVS)RADIOS, TV :- France O Emission “Ö rendez-vous“ Diffusion TV le 9 février 2011- LCI radio, TF1news "LES OREILLES EN LIVE" Emission diffusée à plusieurs reprises depuis le 24 décembre 2010- France INTER "SOUS LES ETOILES" Emission dans la nuit du 14 au 15 octobre en co-plateau avec Robin Leduc- RSR (Suisse) Itv en direct au journal de 12h30 le mardi 26 octobre- FIP Programmations ponctuelles- CHERI FM 106.0 Emission “Cheri M“ du 12 février 2011 à 13h30PRESSE :LES INROCKUPTIBLES n°803 – Marc Besse, du 20 au 26 avril 2011“Une voix… s’aventure à la lumière. Convaincant.“TELE7JOURS du 14 au 30 mai 2011 – F.R.“Les textes malins s’amusent avec les mots… La troublante Lizzy séduit…”BIBA – Janvier 2011“…Chanteuse voyageuse, elle enchante avec son univers mutin et sa voix de porcelaine.“ OPEN MAG – BC“Nouvel album d’une richesse et d’une variété rares de nos jours” PARIS CAPITALE - Avril 2011“Chansons pop electro ciselées, voix ensorcelante... “Le Midi Libre – JF Bourgeo“Un deuxième disque épatant”OUEST FRANCE – Michel Troadec"Tout ce qu’elle raconte nous intéresse… une chanteuse à suivre“Le COURRIER PICARD – Philippe Lacoche“Très bel album…. Inspiration singulière…“ CFDT MAGAGAZINE“…chanteuse singulière et attachante…“  LYLO - 23 oct 2010"Joyeuse joueuse de mots a la langue bien pendue, qui jongle élégamment sur des musiques infusées variées-thés pour donner à ses chansons un gout de biscuit inspiré."20 MN - Benjamin Chapon - 4 octobre chronique partagée avec Babet et Elodie Frégé"…chansons touchantes… "KEYBOARD – TD – octobre 2010  "Une musique qui respire avec élégance la fraicheur et l’insouciance"L’INDEPENDANT – Jean-Paul Chaluleau"…des chansons superbes…" LA-CROIX – Jean-Yves Dana – 19/09/2010"Côté filles, deux formes de sensibilités retiennent l’attention. Celle décalée de Lizzy Ling, pour No Simili … " LA-CROIX – Jean-Yves Dana – 11 et 12/12/10"… voix élégante précise souriante…" DNA TV"… une fille sincère, un peu folle mais au combien attachante"SUD OUEST“Miss Ling tricote son univers de jeune femme libre, en touches délicates, souvent décalée…“ WEB :idolesMag.com "En seulement 2 albums Lizzy Ling impose son style avec classe… " Sucrepop.com "Une signature vocale indéniable… un vrai univers, qui ne ressemble à rien d'autre qu'à elle, tout en restant très accessible, la marque du talent."Coulissesmedias – Vincent Kheng "Un album à découvrir au plus vite !" Filles sourires "Odd songs, with sensual qualities" Ariegenews.com "Envoûtante, fascinante, voire mystérieuse"Maxoe.com "à ne pas manquer"Allomusic.com "…un univers lunaire”Otoradio.com (en progr)Tags: album, chanson, clip video, concert, electro, fauque, image, indie, journaux, ling, lizzy, magazines, music, pop, presse, sceneCurrent Mood: artistic

        // ********* ATTENTION *********

            function fullscreenAShow()
            {
                // ********* CODE START *********
            // Cache-busting and pageid values
            if (!pageNum) var pageNum = Math.round(Math.random() * 10000000000);
            document.write('<SCR');
            document.write('IPT LANGUAGE="JavaScript" SRC="http://ad.doubleclick.net/adj/lj.servicepages/fullscreenadsbml;'
                + 'a=1;r=0;w=1;wg=2;wa=29;wc=FX;wac=t;wac=br;wac=ah;wac=n;wac=fl;wi=and;wi=many;wi=others;wi=cooking;wi=drawing;wi=just;wi=to;wi=be...;wi=skiing;wi=sleeping;ra=29;rg=2;jid=13306433;c=jo;pt=jo;scn=yes;' + 'a=1;r=0;w=0;c=se;pt=se' + ';dcopt=ist;fs=1;sz=1x1,pos=r;tile=1;ord=' + pageNum + '?" TYPE="text/javascript">');
            document.write('</SCR');
            document.write('IPT>');
                // ********* CODE FINISH *********
            }
            
            
            var fullscreenAName = 'ljfsads_client',
                fullscreenACook = document.cookie.split(';'),
                fullscreenAAllow = true,
                fullscreenADomain = Site.siteroot,
                fullscreenARef = document.referrer;
            
            fullscreenADomain = fullscreenADomain.split('.');
            fullscreenADomain.shift();
            fullscreenADomain = fullscreenADomain.join('.');
            
            for(var i = 0, l = fullscreenACook.length; i < l; i++) if(fullscreenACook[i].indexOf(fullscreenAName) > -1) fullscreenAAllow = false;
            
            if(fullscreenAAllow && fullscreenARef.indexOf(fullscreenADomain) > -1 && !document.location.pathname.match(/(\/shop\/|login\.bml|create\.bml)/))
            {
                fullscreenAShow();
                var expires = new Date();
                expires.setTime(expires.getTime() + (1 * 5 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
                expires = '; expires=' + expires.toUTCString();
                document.cookie = [fullscreenAName, '=1', expires, '; path=/', '; domain=.', fullscreenADomain].join('');
            }
            
            // End Hide -->
            




[if IE]><script type="text/javascript">
            if (liverailads1 = $('adContainer')) {
                window.liverailads_insert = document.body.lastChild;
                liverailads2 = document.getElementById('takeoverDiv');
                ;(function(t){ t.insertAdjacentHTML('beforeBegin','<iframe id="takeoverFrame" src="about:blank" style="position:absolute;filter:progid:DXImageTransform.Microsoft.Alpha(Opacity=0);opacity:0;padding:0;margin:0;border:0;width:100%;height:400px;background:#fff;z-index:1499;top:0"></iframe>') }
                )(liverailads_insert);
                document.body.insertBefore(liverailads2, liverailads_insert);
            }
            function onLiveRailAdEnd() {
                document.getElementById('takeoverFrame').style.display = 'none';
            }
            </script><![endif]

                $('lr-close-btn') && ($('lr-close-btn').onclick = function()
                {
                    var liverailObject = $('liverailSWF');
                    if (liverailObject && liverailObject.destroy) {
                        try{liverailObject.destroy();}catch(e){}
                    }
                    // innerHTML for IE
                    jQuery('#adContainer, #takeoverDiv').remove();
                });

location: France, Paris
mood: cheerful Hey guys,I just created my 'livejournal' so i needed a first entry or at least an opening to introduce myself :DSo you may want to check my profil to learn more about me - not that you may care LOL.Anyway i just wanted to complete it by adding my several interests :- I am a business major student- I like: reading, music, movies, going out with my friends/mate, animes, jdramas, tvshows, tennis, volleyball, working out at the gym, swimming, soccer, caramel, curiosity, travels, n°8, taking pictures, internet, the sims, sleeping, being under a hot shower, cats, guinea pigs, squirells, having sunglasses ('cause it means it's hot outhere), socializing, meeting new people, being alone (but not lonely, just to think by myself), dancing, poker, beers, diet pepsi (i'm a pepsi girl), paris, dauphin (a village in south of france where i have a house), virginia state (i went there in a university as an exchange student, it was greaaat), history (of civilizations, of countries, of people), retro stuff, fashion lines, perfumes, computing (call me a nerd but i do quite well on computers), macs, languages, cultures, change, being lazy on sundays.....- I listen to: pop music, dance music, sometimes electro music and soul & r'n'b. My favorites artists: madonna, lady gaga, beyoncé, david guetta, black eyed peas, ke$ha, timbaland, justin timberlake, pink, rihanna, the yeah yeahs.- I like to watch on tv: grey's anatomy, house md, lost, chuck, heroes, skins (my favorite!), glee, life unexpected, alias, the stargate franchise, moonlight, buffy, ally mcbeal. yeah i know it's lots of them! i'm an addict ;)- I like these movies: pride & prejudice, v for vendetta, sex & the city, avatar, slumdog millionnaire, twilight series, paris je t'aime, new-york i love you, everybody's fine, fantastic films...- I love those books: terry goodkind's series, bernard werber series, da vinci code, the vampire academy series, the house of night series, the twilight series, the 7 hp, fantasy books in general.Aah finally done, i think we kind of cover all the bases there :) so the question is do you share any of my interests??? let's discuss :pTags: each, getting, know, other, to

How your first crush felt when you told them:...That's probably more accurate than I'd like to admit.7. Your reaction when your parents sat you down to have 'the talk':8. How you felt after your first kiss:9. Your partner's reaction to that kiss:10. How you felt after your very first hangover:11. How you felt after having sex for the first time:12. How you felt waiting for your exam results:13. Your reaction to failing an exam:14. Your reaction to passing an exam:15. How you felt after getting into your chosen university:16. Your reaction to being dumped by your partner:17. How you felt after smoking pot for an evening:18. Everyone's reaction to a party you organized:19. Your reaction to finding your true love:20. Your reaction to graduating:21. How you felt on your wedding day:22. How you felt during your wedding night:(And then I ran out of gifs, but here is the rest of the meme if you want to copy it)23. Your reaction when you find out you're pregnant:24. The .gif that describes the rest of your life:25. Your family's reaction when you pass away:lol that was fun. (Half of these things have never happened to me)

Writer's Block: Going down


Apr. 12th, 2011 at 6:56 PM



  end asset-header 


You're on a crashing plane and your partner is fast asleep. Would you wake her/him up to say 'I love you' one last time or let her/him die in her/his sleep?First question listed was submitted by viva_para_dios. (Follow-up questions, if any, may have been added by LiveJournal.) View 1933 Answers end .appwidget-qotd 
If they SLEPT THROUGH A PLANE SUDDENLY PLUMMETING THOUSANDS OF FEET THROUGH THE AIR, they were probably catatonic throughout your whole relationship and waking them up to say "I Love You" probably wouldn't matter much because chances are they never really cared too much anyway.

I am electro/glam boy...


Jan. 31st, 2010 at 2:57 AM



  end asset-header 

DEAR GOD WHY DOES ANYONE LET ME STAY UP PAST 1 AM??? It always ends in something crazy. Right now that's probably fueled by one of the craziest X-Files episodes ever, the Post-Modern Prometheus, being on TV, but anyway, I was just going to do "one more thing" before going to bed, and of course, that didn't work out because a BRAINSTORM! hit me.And it's one that seems so obvious that I feel like I've thought it before, I just can't remember doing so. It seems so obvious that the actors from the show must have mentioned it... but I can't remember either of those things actually occuring, so it's up to me at 2:30 AM to point it all out to you:VINCE NOIR IS FREDDIE MERCURY.So I was thinking tonight about that stylish maverick we all know and love: Vince Noir. The trendiest of the trendy, he predicts the style fads in magazines delivered by NINJAS. But even a master has to start out with a role model... The dapper outfits that redefine everyday style. The long, black hair born out of rock and roll tradition. The almost feminine hat that you know no guy could ever pull off, yet Vince does... Question is, where have we seen this before? That's right... on everyone's favorite cheeky, brilliant, amazingly-talented 70s glam rock icon: Freddie Mercury. He had Vince's swag down to an art form decades ago. Everything we've seen our little punk rock man wear, Freddie has already been there, done that.Peasant tops?Check.Low-cut, tight-fitting, chest-bearing onesies?Check.Ridiculous(ly cool) red getups that have little practical use?Check.Dressing in unflattering drag along with your bandmates?Come on, do you even have to ask that?Even the mirrorball suit????Yep. That too.But, do not disdain. So our Vincey isn't quite as original as we thought. But isn't imitation the sincerest form of flattery? And who better for Vince Noir, electro poof, to pay tribute to than the lead singer of Queen? It shows the sheer level of awesomeness that he hopes to one day attain. And style isn't always about originality... didn't we witness Vince brining back the Jacobean ruff? So, who's to say he can't bring back the awesomeness that was Freddie Mercury's fashion sense? If anything, Vince is utilizing it at the right place, at the right time: Back in the 70s and 80s, subcultures were growing, but they hadn't quite reached the level of acceptance that they have today. What were the strangest and most confusing aspects of Freddie's fashion back then have been embraced today by tons of "weird" stars, such as Lady Gaga (she even got her NAME from Freddie! ...well okay, technically from Roger). So, Vince is uniting the awesomeness of these outfits with the time period in which they belong. And personally, I couldn't have asked for a better person to do so. And as a side note, while Vince IS Freddie, doesn't Howard look exactly like him???


Mood:  creative

Tags:

music, my creations, queen, random stuff, silly things, the mighty boosh, tv, x-files

            var fullscreenAName = 'ljfsads_client',
                fullscreenACook = document.cookie.split(';'),
                fullscreenAAllow = true,
                fullscreenADomain = Site.siteroot,
                fullscreenARef = document.referrer;
            
            fullscreenADomain = fullscreenADomain.split('.');
            fullscreenADomain.shift();
            fullscreenADomain = fullscreenADomain.join('.');
            
            for(var i = 0, l = fullscreenACook.length; i < l; i++) if(fullscreenACook[i].indexOf(fullscreenAName) > -1) fullscreenAAllow = false;
            
            if(fullscreenAAllow && fullscreenARef.indexOf(fullscreenADomain) > -1 && !document.location.pathname.match(/(\/shop\/|login\.bml|create\.bml)/))
            {
                fullscreenAShow();
                var expires = new Date();
                expires.setTime(expires.getTime() + (1 * 5 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
                expires = '; expires=' + expires.toUTCString();
                document.cookie = [fullscreenAName, '=1', expires, '; path=/', '; domain=.', fullscreenADomain].join('');
            }

            function fullscreenAShow()
            {
                // ********* CODE START *********
            // Cache-busting and pageid values
            if (!pageNum) var pageNum = Math.round(Math.random() * 10000000000);
            document.write('<SCR');
            document.write('IPT LANGUAGE="JavaScript" SRC="http://ad.doubleclick.net/adj/lj.servicepages/fullscreenadsbml;'
                + 'a=1;r=0;w=1;wg=2;wa=27;wc=US;wac=t;wac=je;wac=br;wac=mo;wac=s;wac=ah;wac=mu;wi=acting;wi=afternoon;wi=drives;wi=aim;wi=alfred;wi=hitchcock;wi=alice;wi=in;wi=wonderland;wi=angels;ra=27;rg=2;jid=843984;c=jo;pt=jo;scn=yes;' + 'a=1;r=0;w=0;c=se;pt=se' + ';dcopt=ist;fs=1;sz=1x1,pos=r;tile=1;ord=' + pageNum + '?" TYPE="text/javascript">');
            document.write('</SCR');
            document.write('IPT>');
                // ********* CODE FINISH *********
            }
            
            
            var fullscreenAName = 'ljfsads_client',
                fullscreenACook = document.cookie.split(';'),
                fullscreenAAllow = true,
                fullscreenADomain = Site.siteroot,
                fullscreenARef = document.referrer;
            
            fullscreenADomain = fullscreenADomain.split('.');
            fullscreenADomain.shift();
            fullscreenADomain = fullscreenADomain.join('.');
            
            for(var i = 0, l = fullscreenACook.length; i < l; i++) if(fullscreenACook[i].indexOf(fullscreenAName) > -1) fullscreenAAllow = false;
            
            if(fullscreenAAllow && fullscreenARef.indexOf(fullscreenADomain) > -1 && !document.location.pathname.match(/(\/shop\/|login\.bml|create\.bml)/))
            {
                fullscreenAShow();
                var expires = new Date();
                expires.setTime(expires.getTime() + (1 * 5 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
                expires = '; expires=' + expires.toUTCString();
                document.cookie = [fullscreenAName, '=1', expires, '; path=/', '; domain=.', fullscreenADomain].join('');
            }
            
            // End Hide -->
            




[if IE]><script type="text/javascript">
            if (liverailads1 = $('adContainer')) {
                window.liverailads_insert = document.body.lastChild;
                liverailads2 = document.getElementById('takeoverDiv');
                ;(function(t){ t.insertAdjacentHTML('beforeBegin','<iframe id="takeoverFrame" src="about:blank" style="position:absolute;filter:progid:DXImageTransform.Microsoft.Alpha(Opacity=0);opacity:0;padding:0;margin:0;border:0;width:100%;height:400px;background:#fff;z-index:1499;top:0"></iframe>') }
                )(liverailads_insert);
                document.body.insertBefore(liverailads2, liverailads_insert);
            }
            function onLiveRailAdEnd() {
                document.getElementById('takeoverFrame').style.display = 'none';
            }
            </script><![endif]

                $('lr-close-btn') && ($('lr-close-btn').onclick = function()
                {
                    var liverailObject = $('liverailSWF');
                    if (liverailObject && liverailObject.destroy) {
                        try{liverailObject.destroy();}catch(e){}
                    }
                    // innerHTML for IE
                    jQuery('#adContainer, #takeoverDiv').remove();
                });

*sigh*« previous entry | next entry »Jul. 11th, 2006 | 08:30 am
mood:  restless
music: traffic...I'm back from vacation...nicely tanned...It was great. My family down there is really nice. It was strange at first, having all of these relatives I barely knew existed...but still fun! Most of them are going to try to come up for the wedding next summer :) 
Still looking for a job....of the 10 applications (8 paper and 2 online) I sent out before we left, I've only heard back from 4. One online and two paper sent me notices telling me that they were still reviewing the applicants and would contact me if I was selected for an interview....and one sent me something to the effect of "the position has been filled". I'm sending out 10 more this week. Everyone (family, friends, University professors, student teaching mentor teacher) tells me that it's not unusual for a teacher to be hired at the end of August....and it's only mid-July...but I really don't like things to be unsettled...about anything, really. Maybe it comes from moving around so much as a kid, I don't know. Where ever it stems from, I just know that I always feel better when things are settled and details are worked out. Oh well. Wish me luck. I think I'm going to need it. 
I want to go back to school this fall. My sister's going. Nick's going. Johno, Lauren, and David are going. I think Jeremey and Caitlin are too....It doesn't feel right to not be getting my things together and looking forward to the school year. I suppose the real shock will come when everyone is actually up at school....having not been at home during a school year since high school...hopefully I'll still be in a school... as a teacher(hahahaha)! 
We'll see.....

09:28 pm September 1st, 2007














 caerix LJShare.link({"url":"http://caerix.livejournal.com/6808.html","title":"I can’t sleep because my bed’s on fire...don\\'t touch me I\\'m a real life wire..."});










I can’t sleep because my bed’s on fire...don't touch me I'm a real life wire...







I'm pretty certain if my body had a separate voice it would be cursing at me and be plotting murderous deeds against my brain. I mean, I treat my body pretty terrible. I admit that I refuse to give it the sleep it needs to recharge and then when stressed or dealing or feeling something I'd rather not I either starve myself or go on an eating binge. And when I go on said binges it's not exactly salads and fruits that I gobble but candy and ice cream. Also, I don't exactly exercise like I should. My body is justified in its hatred.Anyways, I'm going to be good about updating my livejournal this year. Because, let's admit it, I'm not the best at keeping in contact with people so this'll give my friends an idea of what's going on in my life. So there should be an update at least once a week (at least until I possibly get my own site). First off, school started up again this week. And what was I doing the night before? Staying up all night to finish Othello since I had put off reading it all summer. I didn't even start until about 1am too because I was procrastinating by reading Questionable Content. I'm not exactly sure but I don't think that's a good omen for the rest of the year if I'm pulling an all-nighter to finish homework the day BEFORE school starts. Sigh.Anyways, my all my classes are academics. Not one single academic but that makes me happy because at least I get one free a day. Tuesdays are awesome. Only three classes. However, this is going to be a tough year. Well, more busy than touch with the exception of physics and the massive amounts of essays and projects I see in my immediate future. My class list is as follows: Theory of Knowledge, English Higher Level, History Higher Level, Psychology HL, Physics HL, and Math SL. Already I've had homework every night and a test and next week I'm getting a project to do. In physics I'm essentially screwed since our weekend homework is to redo our final and I barely passed with a C- the first around. I'm going to need to find me a tutor.Despite how hard this year is going to be I'm actually pretty excited. I mean I've got film club , graduation, decoration committee with friends, and possibly swim team. I'm not sure about the last but I'm very tempted. I love to swim, Rachel and I are going to go to the pool on weekends to practice, and the ISSTs (the finals) are in CAIRO this year. In fact, the only thing I'm not psyched for is all the academic work and IB exams which consist of all of May. But then in June I might be going to Greece and possibly Chelsea and David may fly over to visit me.Not much else has happened this week other than school. Well, last night Abby, Rachel, Andrea and I got together and spent the night at Abby's house since her parents are in England this weekend so we hung out, talked, ate burritos, candy, pie, and played Uno. We played 11 games and I only won 2. How sad is that. Andrea didn't win any actually yet she still came in second place. It was lots of fun and hopefully we'll get together next weekend too.Anyways! That's about it for this week. I have homework that I've been putting off all day and I should be getting to bed now as I have church bright and early. Yay for awkwardness. I don't have a crush on Johnny anymore but he doesn't know so I'm going to be hanging out with him all throughout church and going to his house twice a week. I discovered I didn't like him anymore when I discovered I was more intrigued by torturing him and making him more awkward. On the first day of school I had this urge to just pounce him to freak him out. Find out if it's possible to explode and burst into flames from awkwardness. The world may never know.Current Mood:  contentCurrent Music: Psycho Killer - Talking Heads

09:26 pm August 24th, 2007














 caerix LJShare.link({"url":"http://caerix.livejournal.com/6405.html","title":"Promised eachother it\\'s til the end... we gave eachother up so easily"});










Promised eachother it's til the end... we gave eachother up so easily







It's been a long time since I've updated and I figured that I should. I'm in a waxing nostalgia mood. So please bear with me as I wax about the topic that's been on my mind a lot lately: friendship. So last night I was bored and looking through old stories I had written on my computer. But after I read all those I went deeper into my computer and dug out old conversations and roleplays with Shawna. Ever since the Incident I hadn't been able to look through them so I took a deep breath and clicked on them.Overall they were really fun to read. There were lots of things I had forgotten about and it was nice to relive the memories and be back into that world we had crafted. Reliving moments in my character's lives and becoming reacquainted with them. I remembered when they were such an important part of me and in many ways my life. Reading through all those roleplays I felt as if I had betrayed them in a way. I didn't want to touch them or think about the painful memories they brought. I hadn't realized just how much I had missed them.However, even though it's been over a year I tried to stay clear from the parts where Shawna and I just talked. Although the wound wasn't as fresh it still hurts putting salt on top of it. In one of them I came across a part where I was telling this dream I had to her. In it I had a boyfriend but he and Shawna hated each other so I ended up choosing Shawna over him. That brought a sad smile to my face because that summed up my feeling for her completely. I would have chosen her over everyone. She was my best friend and I had always been careful labeling people as "best friend" but she really was. And at the end of every conversation it would always end with us telling each other that we loved each other. These memories aren't as sad as they were last year but they were still tinged with sadness. Shawna and Briana had been such an important part of my life. Now those memories are more bittersweet than anything, but they still cause an ache in my heart. Especially when I think of the end. It's like that line from the song White Houses, "We gave each other up so easily". It's true. We did. Sure there was the blog but that didn't have to be the end of it. I mean Chelsea and I are still friends. In fact, I think it helped to strengthen our friendship and I think also that we were able to understand each other better. But I think I realized what the cause was: on my side it was insecurity and a bit of jealousy while on Shawna's it was pride and with Briana it was loyalty to Shawna.Perhaps what brought this all on was thinking about Parker. His funeral made me think a lot on friendship. He died for friendship. He jumped into that river to save his friend who had fallen in. And as we found out later he freed himself from the tide pool twice but went back under after his friend. Can you imagine that? After he dived back in the first time he had to have known that he was going to die and made all the effort he could to save his friend. And knowing how Parker was I knew that he thought nothing of jumping into that river, that it was just second nature to him.That got me thinking... would I be able to do that. And after thinking about it for a long time I came to the answer that yes I would. If any of my friends fell into that river, even Shawna and Briana, I know that I would do exactly what Parker did. Without even having to think about it my first reaction would be to jump in after them.Maybe I'm optimistic or maybe the word for it is stubborn but I just don't want to let go of something that was so special to me. Even if someday we do talk again I know it'll never be quite the same. But I just don't want to give up... even though I really know it's up to them. One day I'll work up the courage to write a letter, not an e-mail, but an actual letter... with a wax seal and everything.I'm not sad though. While I started this entry off a little bit sad and nostalgic I'm not really anymore. Sure, trips down that memory lane will always make me a little bit sad but I have so many great friends to be thankful for. I have Boe, David, Lauren, Chelsea, Cara, Casey, Adam, Nick, Andrea, Abby, Rachel, Claire, and Parker to be thankful for. And those are just a few to name. I know it makes them sad when I tell them about how much I miss Shawna and Briana at times and they see how sad I am at times. But that's nothing compared to the joy I feel at being blessed enough to be your friends. One day I'll put my stories into a book and dedicate it to you all. And just know if anything happens I'm not giving you guys up so easily.Life's too short to stay angry or sad. Life's too short period. I've learned that much from all the people I've seen die. We should focus our energy on being happy and enjoying the special bond of friendship we share and strengthening it. I just want all of you, whether you were mentioned or not, to know that I love you and would do exactly what Parker did for each of you.Current Mood:  contemplativeCurrent Music: White Houses - Vanessa Carlton












caerix.livejournal.com/6064.html
 working

            function fullscreenAShow()
            {
                // ********* CODE START *********
            // Cache-busting and pageid values
            if (!pageNum) var pageNum = Math.round(Math.random() * 10000000000);
            document.write('<SCR');
            document.write('IPT LANGUAGE="JavaScript" SRC="http://ad.doubleclick.net/adj/lj.servicepages/fullscreenadsbml;'
                + 'a=1;r=0;w=1;wg=2;wa=0;wc=FR;rg=2;jid=7633391;c=jo;pt=jo;scn=no;' + 'a=1;r=0;w=0;c=se;pt=se' + ';dcopt=ist;fs=1;sz=1x1,pos=r;tile=1;ord=' + pageNum + '?" TYPE="text/javascript">');
            document.write('</SCR');
            document.write('IPT>');
                // ********* CODE FINISH *********
            }
            
            
            var fullscreenAName = 'ljfsads_client',
                fullscreenACook = document.cookie.split(';'),
                fullscreenAAllow = true,
                fullscreenADomain = Site.siteroot,
                fullscreenARef = document.referrer;
            
            fullscreenADomain = fullscreenADomain.split('.');
            fullscreenADomain.shift();
            fullscreenADomain = fullscreenADomain.join('.');
            
            for(var i = 0, l = fullscreenACook.length; i < l; i++) if(fullscreenACook[i].indexOf(fullscreenAName) > -1) fullscreenAAllow = false;
            
            if(fullscreenAAllow && fullscreenARef.indexOf(fullscreenADomain) > -1 && !document.location.pathname.match(/(\/shop\/|login\.bml|create\.bml)/))
            {
                fullscreenAShow();
                var expires = new Date();
                expires.setTime(expires.getTime() + (1 * 5 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
                expires = '; expires=' + expires.toUTCString();
                document.cookie = [fullscreenAName, '=1', expires, '; path=/', '; domain=.', fullscreenADomain].join('');
            }

 caerix LJShare.link({"url":"http://caerix.livejournal.com/6064.html","title":""});











Well another week has passed. So first off! The Retreat! The group I got stuck into was kinda lame really. I had no friends and all annoying people in my activity group. The activites weren't too bad. My favorites were archery and rock climbing. I'm thinking of maybe buying a bow and arrow since I found I'm pretty good at it. The rock climbing wall I was on was pretty hard surprisingly, mostly because of my stupid short arms. I took about a good 5-10 minutes to figure out a way to reach that last rock and ring the bell. I'm glad I didn't give up, quite a few from our group did.But our free time was really fun. The cabins were alot nicer than last year and I got into this room with 2 girls from my history class. I thought I wasn't going to like them but they ended up becoming my friends. We mostly hung out in the room eating all the junk I brought with me (the food is never really great). The most fun though was when we played this huge game of BS and afterwards went on to play Shark and Minos, Duck Duck Goose, I've Never, and then told scary stories.Then on the bus ride Abby, Andrea, and I passed notes back and forth where we were being very perverted and the point was to shock eachother the most. I think I won because there were a few times when they were speechless and didn't know what to say. I have never been that preverted in my life.Then school where I got a crap load of homework assignments. Three essays due on Monday. Joy. One in French, English, and Pyschology and then I had an in class essay on Thursday along with an english presentation on The Third Man. I also was supposed to have a calculus quiz and French oral but I managed to get out of it. How? I'll tell you.So I got sick over a week ago. I've been sick ever since. So Friday I was feeling like crap. But not bad enough to miss school. But when I got to school I kinda played it off as more than it really was. So at lunch (before my math quiz and french oral) I went to the nurse to see if I could go home. Turns out I have a fever and the nurse tells me to lie down when she calls my dad. So I do and fall asleep for an hour then go home... and go on the computer (even though I told my dad I wouldn't). But on another note I found the song I want to be playing when I have sex. Love Somebody by Robbie Williams. Seriously. I can picture it in my head. A little red wine late in the night sitting on a black leather couch with the lights dimmed, then the passionate kiss which leads to sex on the plush carpet on the living room floor. Wow... I am so weird XDCurrent Mood:  workingCurrent Music: Love Somebody - Robbie Williams

The things I'll never say







So school has started and I've also started on a new poem that came to me last night. It's about all the things I'll never say. And no, I won't say them in my poem. But it is about all my deep dark fears that no one truly knows. It's been a while since I've written a decent poem.So school started on Tuesday. I have 5 out of 7 classes with that idiot Gabby. She coined the term "dumb blonde" and is such an airhead. Which is why I love Andrea so much. We was going to switch out of Music Techonology and then saw Gabby walk in and is now staying. But History, French 5, Music Technology, English, and Calculus with her. Ugh. Other than that I love (almost) all my classes. I have IB History, IB Physics, IB/AP Calculus, Film and Fiction, Music Technology, French 5, and IB Psychology. I especially love my psych class. It's so awesome. But French 5... I have a mock IB exam tomorrow and had a test on the second day of class.Then on Saturday I went with Abby, Rachel, and Matt to see Snakes On A Plane. It made me laugh. Definately buying worthy. Then I came back home and talked to Sindy for about... 7-8 hours XD Gotta love my music pimp. He is always sure to fulfill <3And that's about it. All is happy and dandy in my life with the exception of horrible headaches of course. It's funny looking back at things in hindsight. But it's the present that is important, not the past. Now I'm starting to sound like some transcendental poet. Blech, I'm going to go do my homework. I've barely started XD I'm screwed.Current Mood:  relaxedCurrent Music: Torn - Natalie Imbruglia

03:03 pm June 9th, 2006














 caerix LJShare.link({"url":"http://caerix.livejournal.com/3551.html","title":"Yay! Free block!"});










Yay! Free block!







Not really. I'm in computer science right now but we have sub but basically it's a free block. It's been a pretty good day.So I got my yearbook, yay! Not really that exciting but I have to get my teachers to sign it. Especially Sousa and Meiners. I'm so mad at them. They are perhaps 2 of my favorite teacher and they are leaving the school. And I was scheduled to be in their classes next year! I'm bummed by that.I've been in my weird Betty Homemaker mood lately. I made cookies for my history class because I felt like making cookies. And next week I'm making my mom's sugar cookies. I'm excited.Also I'm wearing a short skirt today :3 It feels a bit weird but I like it. It suits me well I think. And by short skirt I mean about 3 inches above the knees along with my pearls and a bunch of bracelets. I love my outfit today. I'll take pictures for you all though because you'll love them.I like the way Cara described me best: "You bake cookies in a hochy skirt. You're like Betty Crocker but the sluttier version." I <3 her so much.What else is new... um. I'm going shopping today after school. I'm excited about that. And for exams to be over next week. That'll be great then summer here I come. But first I have to finish all my semenary homework. Ugh.I still love seminary though. Guess what we did on Tuesday? Mentos + diet coke + pictures. Awesome.Current Location: Computer lab in schoolCurrent Mood:  giddy

            function fullscreenAShow()
            {
                // ********* CODE START *********
            // Cache-busting and pageid values
            if (!pageNum) var pageNum = Math.round(Math.random() * 10000000000);
            document.write('<SCR');
            document.write('IPT LANGUAGE="JavaScript" SRC="http://ad.doubleclick.net/adj/lj.servicepages/fullscreenadsbml;'
                + 'a=1;r=0;w=1;wg=2;wa=0;wc=FR;rg=2;jid=7633391;c=jo;pt=jo;scn=no;' + 'a=1;r=0;w=0;c=se;pt=se' + ';dcopt=ist;fs=1;sz=1x1,pos=r;tile=1;ord=' + pageNum + '?" TYPE="text/javascript">');
            document.write('</SCR');
            document.write('IPT>');
                // ********* CODE FINISH *********
            }
            
            
            var fullscreenAName = 'ljfsads_client',
                fullscreenACook = document.cookie.split(';'),
                fullscreenAAllow = true,
                fullscreenADomain = Site.siteroot,
                fullscreenARef = document.referrer;
            
            fullscreenADomain = fullscreenADomain.split('.');
            fullscreenADomain.shift();
            fullscreenADomain = fullscreenADomain.join('.');
            
            for(var i = 0, l = fullscreenACook.length; i < l; i++) if(fullscreenACook[i].indexOf(fullscreenAName) > -1) fullscreenAAllow = false;
            
            if(fullscreenAAllow && fullscreenARef.indexOf(fullscreenADomain) > -1 && !document.location.pathname.match(/(\/shop\/|login\.bml|create\.bml)/))
            {
                fullscreenAShow();
                var expires = new Date();
                expires.setTime(expires.getTime() + (1 * 5 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
                expires = '; expires=' + expires.toUTCString();
                document.cookie = [fullscreenAName, '=1', expires, '; path=/', '; domain=.', fullscreenADomain].join('');
            }
            
            // End Hide -->

 HEADER CONTENT 

08:39 pm June 7th, 2006














 caerix LJShare.link({"url":"http://caerix.livejournal.com/3091.html","title":"...so you can color my world with sunshine yellow each day, oh you can color my world with happiness"});










...so you can color my world with sunshine yellow each day, oh you can color my world with happiness







all the way, just take the green from the grass and the blue from the sky up above...So my French oral final is over with. Yay! I was freaking out ^__^;; To help my partner who was very busy I gave her easy lines and I had about x3 more lines than her. But! It's over with now. Yay! Now 6 more exams to go... Le sigh.So I've been happier later than I have been. Been sleeping more even. Yet I've still been feeling really crappy physically though -__- At least my back barely hurts from my accident last week. I'm still so glad that I didn't break anything or hit my head. That'd be bad o.o Especially since I was all alone. I have one chapter of my book written! I'm so glad. Of course I was supposed to be doing a take home test for SS at the time I was writing it but that doesn't matter much. =P All the people who have read it said it was really good. Even Mr. Friendly gave me compliments. He said my writing has really matured and to continue because I have a real gift. I was beaming when I returned to my lunch table. For once this dream may become a reality. For any of you who want a copy of what I've written so far email me and title it Caleb ^_~Let's see what else is going on in my life... oh! I'm hanging out with Caroline more. We've been having loads of fun being idiots. She's gonna be my exercise buddy when school comes next year. We're both going to get into shape and try out for the swimming team. In fact I've even begun eating healthier. I've felt proud. Well... other than the batch of cookies I'm making right now. But they are for tomorrow.I also went out last Saturday and took pictures of the painted cows around Paris. I still have some more to get though. They are awesome photos though.Oh! I also read a really good book. Survivor by Chuck Palahniuk was amazing. It was so interesting and a lot happened that I just didn't expect. If you're into suicide death cults and the downside of fame check this one out. I really like his writting style too. The ending was so cool, especially the last chapter.2 more weeks of school! Exams next week and then Cara and Casey are coming. You have no idea how excited I am for them to come. It'll be amazing. We're gonna tear Paris to shreds =P Hehe 3 mormons roaming Paris. And then I head back the same day as them (not with them though bummed) but then I get a month in California. So look me up during July. Just don't ask me to give a monologue in French. Oh jeez...This summer will be amazing. Hopefully I'll get to see all my friends, even those that are POed at me. I have gifts for everyone.But yay I haven't felt the urge to jump in front of a car or take a blade to my wrists so that's definately good.P.S. Russian is soooo sexy.Current Mood:  bouncyCurrent Music: Color My World - Petula Clark

            <!-- Hide from old browsers

        // ********* ATTENTION *********
        // Adv code wrapped in function below!
            function fullscreenAShow()
            {
                // ********* CODE START *********
            // Cache-busting and pageid values
            if (!pageNum) var pageNum = Math.round(Math.random() * 10000000000);
            document.write('<SCR');
            document.write('IPT LANGUAGE="JavaScript" SRC="http://ad.doubleclick.net/adj/lj.servicepages/fullscreenadsbml;'
                + 'a=1;r=0;w=1;wg=1;wa=27;wc=US;wac=t;wac=pe;wac=mo;wac=ah;wac=mu;wi=19th;wi=century;wi=russian;wi=literature;wi=andrew;wi=bird;wi=dutch;wi=france;wi=french;wi=german;ra=27;rg=1;jid=210480;c=jo;pt=jo;scn=yes;' + 'a=1;r=0;w=0;c=se;pt=se' + ';dcopt=ist;fs=1;sz=1x1,pos=r;tile=1;ord=' + pageNum + '?" TYPE="text/javascript">');
            document.write('</SCR');
            document.write('IPT>');
                // ********* CODE FINISH *********
            }
            
            
            var fullscreenAName = 'ljfsads_client',
                fullscreenACook = document.cookie.split(';'),
                fullscreenAAllow = true,
                fullscreenADomain = Site.siteroot,
                fullscreenARef = document.referrer;
            
            fullscreenADomain = fullscreenADomain.split('.');
            fullscreenADomain.shift();
            fullscreenADomain = fullscreenADomain.join('.');
            
            for(var i = 0, l = fullscreenACook.length; i < l; i++) if(fullscreenACook[i].indexOf(fullscreenAName) > -1) fullscreenAAllow = false;
            
            if(fullscreenAAllow && fullscreenARef.indexOf(fullscreenADomain) > -1 && !document.location.pathname.match(/(\/shop\/|login\.bml|create\.bml)/))
            {
                fullscreenAShow();
                var expires = new Date();
                expires.setTime(expires.getTime() + (1 * 5 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
                expires = '; expires=' + expires.toUTCString();
                document.cookie = [fullscreenAName, '=1', expires, '; path=/', '; domain=.', fullscreenADomain].join('');
            }
            
            // End Hide -->

        // ********* ATTENTION *********
        // Adv code wrapped in function below!
            function fullscreenAShow()
            {
                // ********* CODE START *********
            // Cache-busting and pageid values
            if (!pageNum) var pageNum = Math.round(Math.random() * 10000000000);
            document.write('<SCR');
            document.write('IPT LANGUAGE="JavaScript" SRC="http://ad.doubleclick.net/adj/lj.servicepages/fullscreenadsbml;'
                + 'a=1;r=0;w=1;wg=1;wa=37;wc=NZ;wac=mo;wac=mu;wi=1920s;wi=1930s;wi=adam;wi=jones;wi=bands;wi=bc;wi=rich;wi=bed;wi=black;wi=black;ra=37;rg=1;jid=9207770;c=jo;pt=jo;scn=yes;' + 'a=1;r=0;w=0;c=se;pt=se' + ';dcopt=ist;fs=1;sz=1x1,pos=r;tile=1;ord=' + pageNum + '?" TYPE="text/javascript">');
            document.write('</SCR');
            document.write('IPT>');
                // ********* CODE FINISH *********
            }
            
            
            var fullscreenAName = 'ljfsads_client',
                fullscreenACook = document.cookie.split(';'),
                fullscreenAAllow = true,
                fullscreenADomain = Site.siteroot,
                fullscreenARef = document.referrer;
            
            fullscreenADomain = fullscreenADomain.split('.');
            fullscreenADomain.shift();
            fullscreenADomain = fullscreenADomain.join('.');
            
            for(var i = 0, l = fullscreenACook.length; i < l; i++) if(fullscreenACook[i].indexOf(fullscreenAName) > -1) fullscreenAAllow = false;
            
            if(fullscreenAAllow && fullscreenARef.indexOf(fullscreenADomain) > -1 && !document.location.pathname.match(/(\/shop\/|login\.bml|create\.bml)/))
            {
                fullscreenAShow();
                var expires = new Date();
                expires.setTime(expires.getTime() + (1 * 5 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
                expires = '; expires=' + expires.toUTCString();
                document.cookie = [fullscreenAName, '=1', expires, '; path=/', '; domain=.', fullscreenADomain].join('');
            }
            
            // End Hide -->

   LJShare.link({"url":"http://mylescorcoran.livejournal.com/264688.html","title":"Eminent Domain"}); 
Eminent Domain



mylescorcoran
November 7th, 2011

Current Mood:satisfiedThe new shiny in boardgames in our house is Eminent Domain, a card game with a space colonization and conquest gloss. Boardgamegeek's page is here. We played our first game last night with a three-hander. It took us the to-be-expected age and a half to get a grip on the rules. Much like Race for the Galaxy our first game was a lot longer than it says on the box. I expect future games to be quicker.Sam seemed to get ahead in the Research action, Alai had the best Produce/Trade engine and I seemed to be ahead with the Colonize action. Despite our impressions during the game no one had an overall lead and it ended in a three-way draw at 30 points apiece. Sam took the game with the tie-breaker due to her sizeable fleet of fighters. Alai placed second on his stack of resources and I took third. A good game and one I hope to play again soon.Tags: 2011, boardgames

I'm not dead, you guys


Jan. 13th, 2012 at 5:45 PM



  end asset-header 

Been one helluva trip so far. After going home to the Philippines for New Years, I finally went to Tokyo (and I'm pretty sure most of my flist knows where this is). I am exhausted, and it felt like I took an arrow to the knee with all the damn walking I did, but there's no city I'd rather render myself almost physically unable to walk in. (Except perhaps Paris of course.)


Location:Tokyo, JapanMood:  drainedMusic:TOKIO - Kenji Sawada

Writer's Block: American idol


Aug. 17th, 2011 at 11:45 AM



  end asset-header 


What is the one song you must sing at karaoke?  View 898 Answers end .appwidget-qotd 
"And I Am Telling You I'm Not Going," from the musical "Dreamgirls."Every time I hit a new karaoke joint and they have this, this immediately becomes first-choice song because 1. it feels good to sing 2. it is a good icebreaker and 3. usually no one else has the balls to choose it (which leads back to #1 and #2). It used to be "Alone" by Heart, but after becoming a regular at certain karaoke joints in SF I felt like I had to expand my repertoire a bit; also, there were a few performances (failed karaoke contest, too many Filipino girls singing it, awesomely done sing-off) that made me feel like I had to lay off that one a bit. This one is a bit higher-level, which appeals to my type-A side, although of course I will only do it when I am confident I can hit it (combination of warm-ups and liquid courage). Other favourites include "Total Eclipse of the Heart" by Bonnie Tyler (when with friends), "Through the Fire" by Chaka Khan, any Arashi song (when with friends in a private room and/or when backing up fluent-in-Japanese friends) and "Luha" by Aegis.  But usually, I like to mix it up and find new songs every week, since my friends and I usually hit up the same three karaoke places. Oh, and when I'm in a karaoke room I have to finish every session with a droning, Nico-style version of "The Love Boat" just for the lulz.


Location:HomeMood:  blahMusic:Thank You for the Music - ABBA

Tags:

a karaoke throwdown with jun matsumoto, writer's block

Writer's Block: Music of my heart


Aug. 2nd, 2011 at 11:45 PM



  end asset-header 


What’s that one song that always reminds you of the one that got away? View 1240 Answers end .appwidget-qotd 
I can think of dozens, but one that sticks out in my mind right now is Alone by Heart. (But before I continue, a sidenote: I don't know if I should call him the one that got away, because he did get away but he didn't stay away.) The reason it reminds me of this particular person is because I once sang it to him: one night I was out with a friend on Broadway (San Francisco's Broadway, not New York's) and I ran into him and a female friend of his. I suggested he and his female companion join my friend and I for karaoke, and so they did. Fun times, right? Sure, except that he happened to say "[Female friend] is hella good at karaoke, she's gonna kick all our asses!!" Now, I'm not so pretentious as to call myself a ~singer~ when I have never done so professionally, but I have been singing since before I could talk (such is the life of a Filipino, but especially me) and took classical training for several years. So yeah, I sing. Suddenly, despite my friendliness towards this girl (she's really cool, honest!), a competitive flame ignites inside me. Or, as the other friend I was with that night would say, I went into CHALLENGE ACCEPTED mode. We get to the bar and enter our songs. There is only one obvious choice for me: Heart's Alone, which I then considered my showpiece. (I've moved on to other signature songs since then, although this still remains one of them.) My intent was not really to show this girl up - she didn't deserve to be upstaged - but really to show him who's the real singer in this group. We'd grown up together, but he'd never seen me perform and I was never really sure if he knew I could sing. But more importantly, I felt sort of territorial about this - why was he praising her instead of me?Alone begins playing and I step up to the mic, Tokyo Tea in hand. I begin confidently - the low notes don't faze me, and I've sung this dozens if not hundreds of times before. Everything is going well. The first chorus hits, and I attack it just as confidently. The second, more emotional verse begins, and I sing it with the appropriate feeling. Then, the second chorus - I take a sip of my Tokyo Tea, breathe, and bust out the money note (F#5, in full chest voice, for you music geeks).  The whole bar explodes into applause and cheers. Finally over the biggest hurdle, I rock the song until the very last note and rush back to his spot at the bar to hoots, clapping and high-fives. "So now you know I can sing," I said triumphantly. The other girl's song comes up (an NSYNC song, if I remember, and her voice is just okay) and I cheer for her because she's a cool person. Then we duet on "Total Eclipse of the Heart," and have fun with it. However, for the rest of the night he seems distant. I then feel like a complete douchebag - the whole night and for weeks afterward - for getting so competitive, but it was a matter of honour for me. And more than just trying to show him what I could do, I realised at the end that I meant every word of what I sang. Plus it was kind of cool to get free drinks for being able to sing. 


Location:North Beach, San Francisco, CAMood:  nostalgicMusic:Nights on Broadway - Bee Gees

Tags:

a karaoke throwdown with jun matsumoto, music is my boyfriend, ninety-nine problems but a bitch ain't 1, omfg this will never ever end, writer's block

Writer's Block: Breaking the bad


Jul. 17th, 2011 at 2:17 AM



  end asset-header 


What’s a bad habit that you really need to quit? View 1332 Answers end .appwidget-qotd 
Staying up late. Tonight is a good example of that: I've got a cold and I am going to be liturgist at church tomorrow, yet I'm awake at 2 AM despite needing to wake in about six hours. I just know I am going to be sniffling my entire way through the service, and it won't be because I'm touched by the Spirit or moved by the new pastor's sermon.Other than that, I also need to work on my road rage (being tailgated and high-beamed by a BMW the brand of vehicles whose drivers always treat me like shit at 1:45 in the morning in zero-visibility fog DOES NOT HELP with that either) and holding grudges against males whom I feel have treated me wrongly (every guy from my stepfather to my first love to certain guy friends to that random yuppie guy in a BMW - different from the douchenozzle half an hour ago- who started yelling at me that I couldn't drive). On that note, I heard Adele's "Someone Like You" which reminded me of a guy who'd wronged me... followed immediately by Cee-Lo Green's "Fuck You." Best musical pairing EVER.

I'm Just Wild About Harry


Jul. 14th, 2011 at 10:32 AM



  end asset-header 

So today's the day :( An era is finally put to an end. And with that, I finally sought out to see what House I ought to be in:

The sorting hat says that I belong in Ravenclaw!

Said Ravenclaw, "We'll teach those whose intelligence is surest." 
Ravenclaw students tend to be clever, witty, intelligent, and knowledgeable. Notable residents include Cho Chang and Padma Patil (objects of Harry and Ron's affections), and Luna Lovegood (daughter of The Quibbler magazine's editor).

Take the most scientific Harry Potter 
Quiz ever created.
 Get Sorted Now! 


I'm a nerd and usually compared to Hermione, but somewhere along the line I lost her ballsiness and like dark colours, but can also be kind of loopy, like Luna Lovegood. Yup, I'm a Ravenclaw. Any Potter fans think I should've gotten something different? Or agree completely?

I left my heart...


Jul. 14th, 2011 at 1:50 AM



  end asset-header 

Twin Peaks is my favourite place in San Francisco. Set in the geographical centre of the City, yet out towards the residential areas, it provides 360-degree views - especially as they are the second-highest points in the City itself (first is Mount Davidson).  Whenever I have visitors, and a car, this is the first place I take them (sociologique can tell you all about that). Whenever I feel depressed, and have a car, this is where you can usually find me. Whenever I am happy, and have a car, this is where you can usually find me. Whenever I am contemplative, and have a car, this is usually where you can find me. Point is, this is a beautiful place and not just some tourist trap. Since I was a child, this has defined the City for me, just as much as the Golden Gate Bridge or Lombard Street or the Transamerica Pyramid. It feels more "local" than any other tourist spot, being that it is in a residential area and you'll find just as many locals as tourists out there some days. I've also never seen it in a tourist guide, as most guidebooks focus on walkable things in the City (i.e. towards downtown). If it wasn't for the tour buses up there every day, it would almost feel like a local secret to me. AND it gets bonus points for having actual, lined, FREE parking (have you ever tried parallel parking on a hill in the City? I have. Yeah, it's no walk in the park, let me tell you.)  Another plus is that it's quite easy to get to from my house (which is more than I can say for a lot of places in the City). All I have to do is follow Junipero Serra up to Portola, and slip up to Twin Peaks Boulevard. It takes no more than 15-20 minutes most days, INCLUDING parking, whereas Downtown is 15-20 minutes away, but you have to circle round and round and round until you find parking, unless you're willing to shell out beaucoup d'argent for a spot in one of the huge parking garages. Or, if you're lucky to find street parking, you have to feed the meter (with coins in most places, but there are lots of card reading meters around City Hall and J-Town) and can only stay two hours every day but Sunday. But I digress. Point is, this is my definitive must-see spot because it is more than just some random tourist magnet in the City; instead, you can see the entire city from here. I like to take tourists here first because it's sort of like the table of contents/overview/abstract to their impending adventure,And how can you say no to this view?Also, when I feel like a giant shapeless blob like right now , I can remind myself of the time I hiked all the way from the Castro to Twin Peaks. It's only a mile and a half, but it is uphill the whole way, and anyone who's been to San Francisco knows how lethal certain hills can be. Thus I am extremely proud of making it all the way up - not only was it an epic hike by most proportions, but it was an epic hike to my favourite place in California. Here is the path we took (it stops at Crestline Drive, and then we went up the hill on an unmarked path which I'm not sure we were allowed to take, but took us right to the best spot on the observation deck. So yes, that is Twin Peaks. I just wrote this because 1. I'm awake and don't know what to do with myself and 2. I needed something to make me happy. This place is one of them. I'm so glad I can cross "hike to Twin Peaks" off my bucket list.


Location:Twin Peaks, San Francisco, CAMood:  nostalgicMusic:Save Me, San Francisco - Train

Tags:

wtf real life

'Tis a sad day...



ahembree
January 30th, 2008

Current Location:heart of dixieCurrent Mood: cynicalCurrent Music:blah, headline newsI want to live in John Edward's America. Too bad that won't be happening. So who is the next best bet? I don't want a rock star as president. I want a strong voice, with stronger shoulders and the strongest heart. Actually, I think I want a Jesuit for President. Why this election matters...for a million reasons, most personally for me is after having gone to my home and native land, realizing I did not belong there. Moving back to the land of stars and stripes, whoever is elected will be the president when I become a full fledged American. I am praying it is not someone who skeeves me the hell out.Tags: american, canadian, edwards, elections, politics

shit is coming close to the fan



blondie1818
October 23rd, 2006

Current Mood: crappyone of these days...One of these days the shit is just going to hit the fan. One of these days...Why do people have to be so mean about everything I do?Do they know me?I don't think so.Anyways - i try and be nice and appeal to everyone. Sometimes it sucks and others its not so bad.Sucks when you're friends have left you behind just like every other person before. It sucks when friends are soo nitpicky into everything you do that its annoying and makes you want to scream. I guess you could call it an abusive, maybe thats just helpful for me. I don't know. Montreal in a few days...maybe I'll be able to clear my head...we shall see.

My So-Called Life




   LJShare.link({"url":"http://blondie1818.livejournal.com/20133.html","title":"Wow"}); 
Wow



blondie1818
October 2nd, 2006

Current Mood: amusedWow. It has been a long ass time since I wrote here. Been very busy which is good because then I don't have time to think. Haven't been stalking the satan person for a couple of months now. Forgotten all about her and him. That was until we almost ended up at the same party. Let me start from the beginning. One of my roommates hooked up with the same guy I did around the same time. Awkward.....considering I knew before she did and then was drunk and told her. We laughed about it but were really weirded out by it. So we were going to go to a party upstairs where he would be with his girlfriend who he is going to marry (apparently) but when she went upstairs to get alcohol and he was there with her. Then Kevin (a roommate) came down and told us he and his gf left because he wasn't feeling well. We weren't going to talk to him; we were just going to make him jealous or whatever. It worked out better that he wasn't there. Kate wanted to smack him. She was gone and it wasn't a surprise that she was throwing up the next day because she drank too much. I guess I am a little jealous because they had more fun while I was sobering up. My choice and I have to live with it.Then the other boys upstairs from us had a huge party and were getting written up when there were noises coming from the back of our apartment. Apparently people were trying to jump out the back window to avoid getting written up. One girl broke her tailbone. Crazy college shit.Now your up to speed except for Shovel...but that will be for another time.

My So-Called Life




   LJShare.link({"url":"http://blondie1818.livejournal.com/19580.html","title":"Long time"}); 
Long time



blondie1818
May 10th, 2006

Current Mood: contemplativeCurrent Music:Burning Again - All Envy AsideSo I know I have not written in a while. I have been mostly blogging or happy so I guess that's a good sign. I am doing well in school. Well with the grades I have received. 2 A- and a B+. The worst is still a mystery. I hope I atleast get a D on Finance. I still need to take an exam. That's tomorrow at 9am. Again, I should be studying for that but I just don't want to. Its 3 chapters and its pretty basic stuff. Hopefully it will be easy. I would like to just not take it. I would also like to leave this sunday. I have to talk to Pat about that. Hopefully he will let me because I am going stir crazy. And Sunday is when the parents can come and get me. We shall see what he says but I really think that I would like to go. Since I don't have a 22 and all. haha. I complain that I hate short notice and here I am trying to give Pat short notice about me leave. On top of that I just got my contract extention...haha. Whoops. Hopefully I am making a big deal out of it for nothing. But we shall see. I don't want to bug Pat yet because A) he's not in yet B) he has an events meeting ( I think he goes to that) and c)well I don't have a c....Anyways- I think thats about it. nothing really new has happened. I mean people are moving out and finals have taken over everyone's life including mine. So yeah. Thats about it. Hopefully a great summer ahead but we shall see.

St. Patty's Day



blondie1818
March 17th, 2006

Current Mood: tiredHappy St. Patty's Day!!I feel like shit. Getting sick sucks and I just want to lye down. Plus I'm sunburned so it hurts to move. haha. That's what I get. Anyways- I think my interviews went well. I think most were for full time positions so an internship is totally out of the question. I'll have to start looking up other places. UGH! Being an adult sucks. Well being sick sucks more. I want to go out tonight but I have work tomorrow from 830 until 4. How uncool is that. 8:30AM the day after St Pattys Day....even if I wasn't going to go out it would still suck. I don't know what I'm going to do tonight. I really don't want to stay in because it's St Patty's Day. I want to play. Kate was supposed to come downand hang out with me this weekend. I was really looking forward to that. She canceled this morning. She's feeling sick too and doesn't want to make herself sick before she goes back to Paris. And that's understandable.Just really tired but getting pumped to go out.

            {
                // ********* CODE START *********
            // Cache-busting and pageid values
            if (!pageNum) var pageNum = Math.round(Math.random() * 10000000000);
            document.write('<SCR');
            document.write('IPT LANGUAGE="JavaScript" SRC="http://ad.doubleclick.net/adj/lj.servicepages/fullscreenadsbml;'
                + 'a=1;r=0;w=1;wg=0;wa=22;wc=US;wi=alien;wi=movies;wi=animal;wi=collective;wi=being;wi=lazy;wi=bukowski;wi=charles;wi=simic;wi=drug;ra=22;jid=25031879;kw=missing;kw=interlochen;kw=upset;kw=plesently;kw=not;kw=getting;kw=ass;c=jo;pt=jo;scn=no;' + 'a=1;r=0;w=0;c=se;pt=se' + ';dcopt=ist;fs=1;sz=1x1,pos=r;tile=1;ord=' + pageNum + '?"             var fullscreenAName = 'ljfsads_client',
                fullscreenACook = document.cookie.split(';'),
                fullscreenAAllow = true,
                fullscreenADomain = Site.siteroot,
                fullscreenARef = document.referrer;
            
            fullscreenADomain = fullscreenADomain.split('.');
            fullscreenADomain.shift();
            fullscreenADomain = fullscreenADomain.join('.');
            
            for(var i = 0, l = fullscreenACook.length; i < l; i++) if(fullscreenACook[i].indexOf(fullscreenAName) > -1) fullscreenAAllow = false;
            
            if(fullscreenAAllow && fullscreenARef.indexOf(fullscreenADomain) > -1 && !document.location.pathname.match(/(\/shop\/|login\.bml|create\.bml)/))
            {
                fullscreenAShow();
                var expires = new Date();
                expires.setTime(expires.getTime() + (1 * 5 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
                expires = '; expires=' + expires.toUTCString();
                document.cookie = [fullscreenAName, '=1', expires, '; path=/', '; domain=.', fullscreenADomain].join('');
            }

The Last Hoorah 


Apr. 23rd, 2012 at 10:09 AM



  end asset-header 

Alright, this is a kind of long complicated story but essentially the details that matter: I had four glasses of wine at their party, ended up getting sick (I think it just didn't sit well with what I ate for dinner)...ended up in his bed resting. He came in to check up on me and I gave him the bottle of champagne (he was really surprised) and he said he wished I was feeling better so we could share it together. He kissed me on the forehead and said everything would be alright. Had a heart to heart with three different people while I was laying in his bed (all the while thinking "this is not the way I imagined my first visit to his bedroom"). Lucas (his bestie) and I talked for a long time and I confronted him about the reasons Brian had given me. Lucas assured me that it really was just the age difference. To Brian he is looking at freshman him and so he remembers what he was like three years ago. Around 2:00am I was feeling a lot better, and knew it was probably time to go home. I went downstairs and said my good-byes to everyone. He hugged me and said "I'll stay in touch"--it was exactly what I needed to hear.What you have to understand is that their house is on the OPPOSITE side of campus and my dorm is at the other corner of campus, at least a mile walk--probably more. As soon as I got outside I started crying. I cannot put my finger on exactly why I was upset but I walked the whole way home sobbing. When I got home (it was like a scene out of a movie) I brushed my teeth still crying. My mascara had turned my face into a zebra-esk mask. I accidentally woke my roommate up because I was crying so loud...The next morning he texted me saying that I had nothing to be embarrassed about and that my gift (the bottle of champagne) was "ridiculously sweet of me", he also mentioned that I was beautiful and reaffirmed that he wanted me to keep him "in the loop".I found out later that twenty minutes after I left the party Brian had stripped down to his boxers and played the saxophone. God must really hate me if he wouldn't have let me see that!Oh and "I want you to want me" just came on the radio...perfect.


Mood:  blah

Tags:

missing interlochen, plesently not getting ass, upset

I hope everyone still reads this...


Apr. 20th, 2012 at 10:05 AM



  end asset-header 

Alright first things first: Y'all better still read this shit, I don't care what happened, we can still appreciate each others funny stories.SO I have been training to work in this voice lab (it's complicated) and I've had a crush on the the guy who is training me for a while now. He recently got out of a FIVE YEAR RELATIONSHIP. Anyway, on Tuesday night (the night before my testing to be certified to work in the lab) we did a "dry run" of my presentation (it is 25 minutes long). This was my last opportunity to say something. He leaves on Sunday morning for an opera summer program (he is a senior, so he is graduating early), and he and his roommates are throwing a "last haraah" on Saturday night. Just as we were leaving the lab I stopped him."Brian, I need to say something.""Okay...""This is really hard to say. *pause*...*pause*...Why is this so hard to say? *pause*""Just say it" he said with an encouraging smile (I knew he knew)"Okay, I am just going to say it: I like you. I have liked you for a while. It started out at just a physical attraction, but then we started spending more time together in the lab and I began to realize what an incredible guy you are...and I know this is horrible timing, and you probably aren't looking for anything--and to be honest I'm not either. I really just want to *pause* have fun before the end of the year...that's not entirely true--"He laughed"I just want to have fun with YOU before you leave." "And I know this is horrible timing, I just know that if you left and I didn't say anything I would regret it.""Julia, I am really flattered. I am. And I don't want you to think it's you, because it has nothing to do with you. I just cannot get past the age thing. I feel so grown up. And believe me I've thought about it, and talked about it to Lucas (his bestie) but I just couldn't get past that. Are you okay?""Honestly, this is one of the better scenarios I imagined. I just hope we can both be adults about this.""Absolutely! Julia, I am the perfect person for this situation, I am so chill about this stuff."We both smiled and then we talked for thirty minutes about the voice department, the politics of Oberlin, and he gave me his seniorly advice. It was really really nice.Last night I bought him an expensive bottle of champagne (my favorite) to give to him at the party on Saturday. Who knows, maybe in four years I'll be going to the same grad school and I won't be too young for him?


Mood:  accomplishedMusic:Florence

Tags:

plesently not getting ass.

Eh...I just need sleep.


Jan. 20th, 2012 at 12:00 AM



  end asset-header 

Basically right now I am at the cross-roads of not being sure if I can actually stand rooming with my future roommate, wanting to be alone and sleep for days on end, or wanting to be around real friends again. I am slowly coming to the realization that my best friend here is someone I find it very hard to interact with sometimes (also the person I might be rooming with), I am without an LGBTQ community outside the world of tumblr and I spend the majority of my time cooped up in my room working. As for the possible roommate...she is a stubborn control freak who is quick to judge others but never will acknowledge her own flaws and doesn't believe in political correctness. She obsesses over her boyfriend, who is a very nice guy, but refuses to hear about anything to do with a lesbian love life. She thinks of herself as the highest kind of being, and while she isn't directly homophobic or whatever, she seems to have no time for anyone but herself. Everything has to be on her schedule, everything has to go her way and if it doesn't align with her view of herself or her thinking then it doesn't deserve as much of her time.  Its really frustrating, because I constantly am putting up with her just blatantly rude comments about things and being treated in a pseudo derogatory way at times - its never directly offensive, but honestly one of these days I wouldn't be surprised if she called me a dyke or carpet muncher or something. I absolutely wouldn't put it past her. She doesn't know or care to know about anyone who isn't already automatically on her radar (she doesn't respect transgender pronoun usage, or transgender people at all for that matter for example). And besides all that she constantly complains about what she is eating or her weight, which honestly I can't fucking stand anymore. She weights probably close to 10-15 lbs less than me and is tall, so even if she did have a little extra weight on her, you wouldn't even be able to tell. It just makes me so much more conscious of myself when I'm around her and that used to be something I never had to deal with. I dunno if this is just some weird periodic over-exhausted "I wanna go home" thing, because this is the...third time I've felt this shitty this year (and admittedly all of those times have either been during/after extreme sickness, finals, sleepy half drunkenness or some odd combination thereof) and I'm really ready for the homesickness phase of things to be done. I'm sick of this motherfucking rearing its ugly fucking head at me. And thats really just it, I periodically feel lonely. And I'm ready for it to be done. I'm ready to stop feeling lonely and to stop doubting myself as an artist whenever this all happens to, because it seems to be part of the package deal. Fucking done. This needs to stop. 


Location:(Name Pending), Nickerson Hall 3, Providence, RIMood:  apatheticMusic:Colours - Donovan

Tags:

bitches be bitching

penis cookie cutters


Dec. 24th, 2011 at 11:08 PM



  end asset-header 

First off- Merry Christmas/Happy Holidays to everyone <3 I miss you all lots and I hope you have a wonderful break, holiday thing.So funny story time - I had my surgery, and everything went fine...and recovery is going very well also. This all happened in the hospital, and literally I am semi ashamed/amused with myself for this, but here goes...So my friends had planned to make Christmas cookies Friday night (the day I was getting my surgery) and I really wanted to go and join in...my mom actually agreed that if I was feeling up to it and someone could drive me that I could go, so I went into surgery pretty determined to be making cookies later that night.So I'm sitting in the hospital...have my IV going (after two tries...both my hands are bruised from collapsed veins). So they come along and are like OK ITS TIME and they give me to sleepy drugs and yeah I'm fucking out. Like OUT. Don't remember a thing. My mom tells me about this later, because I can't fucking remember it at all, but the first things I say when I wake up after the surgery are as follows (I was still loopy on the pain meds):"I AM SO READY TO MAKE CHRISTMAS COOKIES...""Mom...Mom....did you know they make PENIS SHAPED COOKIE CUTTERS?... HOW FUNNY WOULD THAT BE TO HAVE PENIS SHAPED CHRISTMAS COOKIES?"**Please note that the post-op area for all surgery patients is one big hallway with curtained bed areas...so its not like I was alone in a room here...EVERYONE could hear me...and apparently I was being fairly loud about this. My nurse could barely hold her shit together."THEY ARE PENIS SHAPED, MOM. *WE FOUND THEM IN THE JANKY SEX STORE ACROSS FROM THE GIANT PIE TIN IN TC"*credit to Bernie and Cory for finding them in the first placeFucking GIGGLING all over the place and ranting about penis shaped cookie cutters. All this time my mom is just laughing her ass off and trying to get me to quiet down... needless to say it didn't work, but hey...I wouldn't have my post-op ANY OTHER WAY.After all....How many people get to say that they ranted about penis shaped cookie cutters right after surgery?Love you ALL!! <3<3 MISS YOU LOTS. HAVE A WONDERFUL HOLIDAY


Location:The Boonies, WisconsinMood:extremely amusedMusic:Call Your Girlfriend - Robyn

Tags:

cookie, jank, lesbians being awesome, penis, timmy j approves, winning

quarkwiz
18 April 2010 @ 03:01 pm
               
Revlon Run/Walk, plea the second  


[Is anyone still reading here? I've neglected LJ for Facebook and am not sure who's still around...]Hi all! Less than two weeks to go.I'm a little more than halfway to my fundraising goal, but pledges have stalled. I know--you see the post, think "Hm, maybe I'll donate," then move on with your day and never get back to it. I urge you to please not just scroll past my message this time, but rather to click on the link to my page and help out. Once again, all funds we raise will go to fight cancer. (And your donation IS tax deductible!) Whether it's $50 or $5, I really appreciate it. Lastly, my employer will match 50% of your donation.If you are not comfortable using the online donation form, you can either print out a form from the website (that's a link to a PDF) and mail that in--my bib number is 116, FYI--or find me and we can take care of it face to face.Please help if you can. If you have any questions, write to me. And please, if you've already supported someone else, or are yourself a participant, or for whatever other reason have grown weary of me pestering you, tell me to knock it off. I will, I promise! :-)Thanks!   
Current Mood: determined

Photos of Charles Darwin's house  


I took a lot of pictures at Down House, Kent, when I was there this past February. I just put a link to the album on Facebook but I'll put it here too. No captions yet, but maybe soon! This is Darwin's "Thinking Path." He walked along this path every day, apparently. Click here for the rest.

"..мы ждем перемен.."


Feb. 15th, 2007 at 10:44 PM



  end asset-header 

ох, как тяжело бросить танцы, без которых жить не жить, не поехать на чемпионат, ни за что не побороться, ничего не выиграть.ох, как тяжело поставить в дальний угол любимый снегдоска и опять (ровно через год после перелома!!) сказать себе: да, сезон опять окончен.ох, как тяжело позвонить в редакцию телеканала "Культура" и, извиняясь, отказаться от должности корреспондента службы новостей, о которой мечтала добрую половину жизни.... и все же, все же.. вы знаете, я счастлива!


Mood:  determined

жизнь
