About that Linda thing going around. 


Apr. 18th, 2012 at 7:42 AM



  end asset-header 

Wtf now? Petition against someone online? Sorry but it does bring very bad memories here. This is the bad side of kpop coming to the Games of Thrones fandom. I've seen already how it goes when you "petition" against another human being. Jaebum anyone? Block B?I don't do this shit. I'm not here for personal vendettas ok? People have moronic opinions? I just let them have them and call on them about it but that's it. I don't "petition" for them to shut up. Everyone knows already that the girl is racist, homophobic etc. It's a fact so what's the point exactly?People doing this need to sit back and start fucking reflect on what they are doing at this point.

4:29 AM



  end asset-header 

1. Comment on this post with I VOLUNTEER!2. I will give you a letter.3. Think of 5 fictional characters and post their names and your comments on these characters in your LJ/DW.minviendha provided me with "R".- Rickon Stark. Like you were expecting anything else guys ^^. So obvious. It's not really easy to speak about the love you have for such an obscur character in a huge saga like a Song of Ice and Fire but I suppose it's the all potential that makes me even more passionate. I have no idea how this character will grow. He may become a real warrior, or a psychopath, someone who has memories or perhaps none. Right now, Rickon can still be everything and yet we know he will be, no matter what, a ball of fear and broken love. It's beautiful (and now I sound weird ^^). I like how GRRM handled his case. Small touches here and there, like a painting coming very slowly to life. I can't wait for the next book mostly because it will involve Rickon. And I believe in Rickon ^^.- Raskolnikov from Dostoïevsky's Crimes et Châtiments. I think it's fairly known that I love russian litterature. They have intense characters who are so larger than life that they can eat you on the spot. Raskolnikov is like that. He is pain, suffering, will of being more than his man condition. I probably learned more about forgiveness and its cost in Dostoïevsky's novels than in religion to be honest.- Ron Weasley. My favourite character in Harry Potter along Lupin and Luna. I loved him right away, a bit like Harry I have to say. He's a good friend and a good person despite all his defaults. I know the fandom went all anti-Ron after I left it but whatever. Fandom sometimes likes to believe then only can like or care for "perfect" characters. Which is weird.- Rémi. Best rat ever. Best cook too. I'm not huge on Pixar's work but I have to say that Ratatouille was a jewel and when I went to Eurodisney, we had lunch at Ratatouille's restaurant and we saw the (mechanical) rat, it was too cute for words ^^.One of my neighbours's name is Rémi héhé. We already asked him if he knew how to cook but I don't think he ever saw that pixar so he probably didn't get it.- Rose Dewitt Bukater. Because Titanic. Because Kate Winslet and Leo Di Carpaccio (:p). Because she's a kickass woman who went to live her dream and because she's one of the heroin who has the most gorgeous wardrobe ever. Because I'm pumped to watch this again on a big screen. Because if you jump I jump!Et voilà :)!! Oh also Happy birthday ffolks! fallingtowers, , lancelotfan! Have some delicious cake :).

" Things aren't always what they seem."


Feb. 29th, 2012 at 1:02 PM



  end asset-header 

10/02: " Things aren't always what they seem."I always wanted to be a spy.Tinker Tailor Soldier Spy. Tomas Alfredson. European.If you're looking for James Bond or Jason Bourne, pass your way because this has nothing to do with it. The world of John Le Carré's spies is gritty, slow, grey and full of paranoïa. Who to trust? which one to believe? How far are you willing to to to protect the other? I know it's weird to say but the movie was oddly full of love. Of passion in the purest ethymology. As much as every character tries to behave cooly and cold, the passion and love transpire from their every decision, every look, every breath. I loved it. I truly adored that specific point even more than the plot in itself. Not even talking about the cast, the word flawfree was made for it. 17/02: " I'm a bounty hunter now."Well...not a very convincing one.Recherche Bad Boys desesperement aka One for the money. Julie Anne Robinson. USA.Bad isn't even going to cover this mess. I lost 1h35 of my life there. The only good shot about this terrible terrible movie was Heigl's body.18/02: " At last we will reveal ourselves to the Jedi."And may the force be with you.Star Wars I: The Phantom Menace 3D. Georges Lucas. USA.I had a bad memory of this one and I have to say that rewatching it was quite enjoyable this time. Yes Jar Jar Bins is still a moron and that part in Tattoine gets on my nerve but the rest is great. I love Star Wars anyway :p and Darth Maul is SEXY YES I SAID IT!! 24/02: " Did you just kill my wife?"Elémentaire mon cher... y'a jamais eu de Parker pourtant :o.Sherlock Holmes 2- Jeux d'ombres. Guy Ritchie. USA.To be done.

Oh look! A fangirling post! And some meme involving Batman ohhhhh yeah!


Nov. 21st, 2011 at 3:45 PM



  end asset-header 

State of mind those last few hours:  It's been hours since I saw that video from Games of Thrones season 2 and I'm still high on it.  So far so perfect! Of course I have little complains and I will name them but overall STANNIS DAVOS STANNIS STANNIS RENLY WHY BARATHEONS ARE THIS HOT? TYRELL AWESOME!!!! I spent the ENTIRE VIDEO flapping my hands and making ecstatic dolphin noises. It was quite worrying tbh. But there it is!Quick thoughs except I put this under a link for people who want to stay virgin-season2 (you never know...). It's official, I'm in love with Stannis. Real King Lobster should just adopt my bb Rickon and rule Westeros with Davos and Shaggydog. SHOULD BE CANON GRRM *sending waves*.  Tyrell's are beautiful. Even with Dormer looking a lot older than what should Margaery be in the books, I find that the little glimpse we saw works really well. It was tiny seconds but it reassured me just fine.  Melisandre looks so much like I pictured her in that semi-second it's effin scary now :/.  I've seen people complaining about the lack of Jeyne W. and Ygritte. Ok this is where I'm going to rant a bit because it pisses me off actually more than it should and I feel as pressed as a panini about this trivial matter. I am not having a proper Aeron (because that man talking with Theon was certainly not Aeron) while the man is in the books. I am not having the bloody Reeds. So honestly I don't see why I should be flooded with random Jeyne W. who is only mentionned a bit in the books and Ygritte whom I love but only appears in the last chapters of ACOK. I understand people cheering for their underdogs and all but let's keep it real. Am I complaining about not enough Rickon? Nope! While honestly I should.  I don't want this to be taken the wrong way, I don't mind that much Jeyne W.'s arc being expanded. Means more Richard (possibly shirtless or naked) and I adore Oona (The Hour FTW) but I can't with people complaining about lack of them when clearly I'm not having some other canons characters in order to have this storyline. That being said, I would have loved more Brienne, Jaime and Greyjoy. But it's the first teaser and we can't have everything at the same time :p. Patience is a virtue XD.  Three words: Renly. Beard. Crown. Ok now let's count it's way to the awesome: THE HAIR (see how I have my priorities well set?)This proving once again how right I am when I say that Michelle Fairley is the most gorgeous woman on the set of Games Of Thrones (and that's saying a lot because this show is full of insanely pretty people). Also I love how Loras stands around looking gorgeous, hair at full glory! It's good GoT is playing to its strengths.KING CRAZY JOFFUgh if that's the scene where Joffrey says to Sansa that his brother is winning and that she should pay for it.... this is going to be so hard to watch. But the guy playing Joffrey is so good at it, I know I'm going to enjoy every second I'll be able to hate the character in a fierce way. Also the "I'm your future husband so I'm going to point an arrow at you" vibe of this pic is just fantastic. Smooth like chunky peanut butter.Random but I totally love Joffrey's fashion. Yeah yeah shoot me!LIKE A BOSS Excuse you but Davos and Stannis are just too cool for everyone at the moment. According to season 2, if you come from Stormlands then your second name is BAMF. CAN'T SAY I DON'T APPROVE!COOL AWESOME CROWNSBecause don't lie: that's the best crown ever. When I first saw that I was "Renly: A MILLION, The world: 0".STANNIS DILLIANE ANGSTINGOnly rightful king of this realm Y/Y? ♥ ♥ ♥  (I still love you Robb but the lobster is winning some cookies here). This is totally his "Why did the Gods inflicted me with brothers :/"  face ^^.Ok honorable mentions for Theon Greyjoy looking like a true Greyjoy at last! Getting out of Winterfell has been good to him apparently :p  (not going to mention again pseudo-Aeron because obviously not a Greyjoy), Arya being adorable, Samwell having the best expression ever, Melisandre looking like a Vermerr painting for that split of second and Sansa and Tyrion on the same frame. Robb looks very emo-ish which is cool. Jon wants to get deeper and deeper (oh the jokes this is going to bring...) and Littlefinger has some trouble to breathe.Last little thing:SAMWELL'S FACES. ALWAYS PERFECT. HE SHOULD GET ALL THE AWARDS.All in all SQUEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEE \O/! Now it's been days since that meme but there it is at last :p:1. Reply to this post with "CAUSE I'M THE GODDAMN BATMAN," and I will pick four of your icons.2. Make a post (including the meme info) and talk about the icons I chose.3. Other people can then comment to you and make their own posts.4. This will create a never-ending cycle of icon glee. Key words: Rickon and the Chamber of Secrets.Oh Snap dear Tom Riddle. Made by digipacoprIt's one of my multiple Rickon Stark icon. Obviously I'm rooting for him so it's normal to show it. And he wears pretty well that crown. King Rickon is half-a-joke, half not-so-much ^^. I really dig the character and the mystery around him. GRRM did a splendid job with the baby Stark. Also I like to mix fandoms that's why when I saw that text digipacopr put, I instantly tough of Tom Riddle in COS. You know that if Harry had Shaggydog, things might have gone in another direction pretty quickly XD.Key words: Judging you.It's all part of the plot. GRRM. Killing your faves since 1996. Made by onaan.Recent icon. I kept changing the icons for that "Judging you" tag tbh. GRRM is a destroyer of lives so I believe it's adequate here. Also, I'm very fond of his suspenders somehow. Suspenders are cool ^^.Key words: Sanctuary., So french it hurts.House Tyrell. Comme la France d'une certaine manière. Made by wild_plumsTyrell is forever french not only because Highgarden is completely coming from the french landscape but also because Margaery's story is totally taken from les Rois Maudits. Also I wanted a Tyrell icon and a Paris icon so I just mixed the two here. Well of course there's nothing Tyrell in the picture... should have been green tbh. But I like it ^^. It's pretty and girly. I might change though. Also I love the Eiffel tower. I love my city. It's home after all. Can't help it really ^^.Key words:  Hate is such a strong word.And what doesn't kill you only makes you wish it did. Made by triniroslin15I didn't always liked Cat. She made terrible decisions and she's far from being awe-striking but I learned to understand her. What really did the trick I believe in my complete change of heart for her is Michelle Fairley. I find the actress not only so earthly beautiful but with so much restrain and emotions. She plays Catelyn in a way that makes me root for her right away. She had some of the best scenes during season 1 like everything that involved Robb was just heartbreaking. And I dread the day I'll watch the RW with that actress because tears falling down is not even going to cover it. I will be a mess.YOUR TURN!


Mood:  cheerfulMusic:Roch Voisine - Noël Du Campeur

Pourtant tous ce qu’ils avaient fait c’est de s’aimer.



psychoseisblack
May 27th, 2009

Current Mood: angryCurrent Music:cali-Je crois que je ne t'aime plus   Pièce froide et blancheTable de l’enfer,Faible lumière du Paradis,Trop loin il lui est interdit,Blanche était son âme,La pureté la salieContre son grès.Cette nuit à jamais sera inoubliable.Mais la société les a précipités.Ils avaient déjà perdus le control.Ils voulaient juste continué a vivre.Rien n’était sale, tout était pur, leurs cœurs ne savaient rien de leurs méfaits. Et maintenant, là, dans la pièce blanche, sur la terrifiante table trône l’accusation. L’accusation contre le beau, le vrai, le pur.Puis, le verdict est tombé,　«　MORT　» clament les haut-parleurs des raisons externes.Pourtant tous ce qu’ils avaient fait c’est de s’aimer.Mais ils furent séparés, remords et pressions ont tout précipité. Si attirant en ces temps le vide, la fraîcheur de la nuit. La peine choua entraînant son corps et sa pauvre âme.Que ce soit inceste ou mauvais,Que ce soit pressions incontrôlées,Que ce soit un trop grand fossé,Que ce soit une de ces choses insensées,La raison des autres les auras tués.   Pourtant tous ce qu’ils avaient fait c’est de s’aimer.  Tags: aimer, pression, pureté, texte, tout

        // ********* ATTENTION *********

            function fullscreenAShow()
            {
                // ********* CODE START *********
            // Cache-busting and pageid values
            if (!pageNum) var pageNum = Math.round(Math.random() * 10000000000);
            document.write('<SCR');
            document.write('IPT LANGUAGE="JavaScript" SRC="http://ad.doubleclick.net/adj/lj.servicepages/fullscreenadsbml;'
                + 'a=1;r=0;w=1;wg=2;wa=22;wc=FX;wi=cakes;wi=cinema;wi=internet...;wi=jpop;wi=music;wi=tpop;wi=travel;ra=22;rg=2;jid=15505852;kw=everyday;c=jo;pt=jo;scn=yes;' + 'a=1;r=0;w=0;c=se;pt=se' + ';dcopt=ist;fs=1;sz=1x1,pos=r;tile=1;ord=' + pageNum + '?" TYPE="text/javascript">');
            document.write('</SCR');
            document.write('IPT>');
                // ********* CODE FINISH *********
            }
            
            
            var fullscreenAName = 'ljfsads_client',
                fullscreenACook = document.cookie.split(';'),
                fullscreenAAllow = true,
                fullscreenADomain = Site.siteroot,
                fullscreenARef = document.referrer;
            
            fullscreenADomain = fullscreenADomain.split('.');
            fullscreenADomain.shift();
            fullscreenADomain = fullscreenADomain.join('.');
            
            for(var i = 0, l = fullscreenACook.length; i < l; i++) if(fullscreenACook[i].indexOf(fullscreenAName) > -1) fullscreenAAllow = false;
            
            if(fullscreenAAllow && fullscreenARef.indexOf(fullscreenADomain) > -1 && !document.location.pathname.match(/(\/shop\/|login\.bml|create\.bml)/))
            {
                fullscreenAShow();
                var expires = new Date();
                expires.setTime(expires.getTime() + (1 * 5 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
                expires = '; expires=' + expires.toUTCString();
                document.cookie = [fullscreenAName, '=1', expires, '; path=/', '; domain=.', fullscreenADomain].join('');
            }
            
            // End Hide -->

                )(liverailads_insert);

            }

                document.getElementById('takeoverFrame').style.display = 'none';
            }

            function fullscreenAShow()
            {
                // ********* CODE START *********
            // Cache-busting and pageid values
            if (!pageNum) var pageNum = Math.round(Math.random() * 10000000000);
            document.write('<SCR');
            document.write('IPT LANGUAGE="JavaScript" SRC="http://ad.doubleclick.net/adj/lj.servicepages/fullscreenadsbml;'
                + 'a=1;r=0;w=1;wg=2;wa=22;wc=FX;wi=cakes;wi=cinema;wi=internet...;wi=jpop;wi=music;wi=tpop;wi=travel;ra=22;rg=2;jid=15505852;kw=everyday;c=jo;pt=jo;scn=yes;' + 'a=1;r=0;w=0;c=se;pt=se' + ';dcopt=ist;fs=1;sz=1x1,pos=r;tile=1;ord=' + pageNum + '?" TYPE="text/javascript">');

            }
            
            
            var fullscreenAName = 'ljfsads_client',
                fullscreenACook = document.cookie.split(';'),
                fullscreenAAllow = true,
                fullscreenADomain = Site.siteroot,
                fullscreenARef = document.referrer;
            
            fullscreenADomain = fullscreenADomain.split('.');
            fullscreenADomain.shift();
            fullscreenADomain = fullscreenADomain.join('.');
            
            for(var i = 0, l = fullscreenACook.length; i < l; i++) if(fullscreenACook[i].indexOf(fullscreenAName) > -1) fullscreenAAllow = false;

            {

  end asset-header 

I said I would update my journal but I was so busy these days that I totally forgot... >_< I'm supposed to be in holidays but I have to go back to school for X reasons... And it is so cold in France now that I don't want to go outside... I'm happy that I didn't catch a cold yet... ^^ It is very rare to have such temperatures in winter (we had -11C on Sunday morning O_O). It was snowing on Paris the other day, Paris in white was a really beautiful scene to see ^^ The ground was very slippery... XD I'm going to stay at home these days ^^ My lift is out of order and I live at the 6th floor, I'm too lazy to climb up and down... XD It will be repaired for the 5th of February... T.T But I will probably go shopping since the sales began last week in France ^^ I've just finished watching a lot oh things ^^ :I've finished Jin's drama Anego, I just love Jin in black suit ^^ I didn't really like the SP (I generally don't like SP, they are long and are often just flashback of scenes that happen in the drama.... But I will probably change my mind with Code Blue SP ^^)I've also watched HanaKimi SP (finally ! XD, it was in my computer for a long time but I didn't watch it...).KAT-TUN new DVD is my favorite one so far ^^ (Yamapi also appeared in it so what else ? XD) I was just wondering if Ryo attends others Johnnys concert too ? He is so busy with two groups...  I'm curious about who and who are friends in the jimusho XD That's probably why I love Countdown so much ^^ (I was a little disappointed this year but I enjoyed it ^^).I'm planning to buy NEWS Never Ending Wonderful Story concert DVD ^^ But why are NEWS DVD so expensive ??? T.T I'm a poor girl XD It is the first time that I find the DVD zone great, Europe and Japan have the same zone ^^ I have a math and a mechanics test next week T.T Finally, high school mathematics weren't so bad... XD I have no class for the end of this month so I will try to update my journal more often ^^ (If I'm not too lazy ^^)

One more week to go !!!!


Nov. 26th, 2008 at 5:30 PM



  end asset-header 

One more week of school ! I can do it !!! XD And three more weeks before the exams T.T But after I will finally be on holidays ^^ Yattaaaaa !!!! It was snowing in Paris on Sunday ^^ But it was so cold outside !  XD I nearly fall Monday because it was so slippery... I have to draw some industrials plan so I will not write a long entry but since today it's Maru's birthday :Happy birthday Maru ^^ Paaaaaan !!! ^^I will try to get some rest too, so tired these days especially when the trains are full of people every morning T.T

        // ********* ATTENTION *********

            function fullscreenAShow()
            {
                // ********* CODE START *********
            // Cache-busting and pageid values
            if (!pageNum) var pageNum = Math.round(Math.random() * 10000000000);
            document.write('<SCR');
            document.write('IPT LANGUAGE="JavaScript" SRC="http://ad.doubleclick.net/adj/lj.servicepages/fullscreenadsbml;'
                + 'a=1;r=0;w=1;wg=2;wa=32;wc=FR;wi=arts;wi=ballet;wi=economics;wi=france;wi=glenn;wi=gould;wi=music;wi=organ;wi=organists;wi=paris;ra=32;rg=2;jid=14900924;c=jo;pt=jo;scn=yes;' + 'a=1;r=0;w=0;c=se;pt=se' + ';dcopt=ist;fs=1;sz=1x1,pos=r;tile=1;ord=' + pageNum + '?" TYPE="text/javascript">');
            document.write('</SCR');
            document.write('IPT>');
                // ********* CODE FINISH *********
            }
            
            
            var fullscreenAName = 'ljfsads_client',
                fullscreenACook = document.cookie.split(';'),
                fullscreenAAllow = true,
                fullscreenADomain = Site.siteroot,
                fullscreenARef = document.referrer;
            
            fullscreenADomain = fullscreenADomain.split('.');
            fullscreenADomain.shift();
            fullscreenADomain = fullscreenADomain.join('.');
            
            for(var i = 0, l = fullscreenACook.length; i < l; i++) if(fullscreenACook[i].indexOf(fullscreenAName) > -1) fullscreenAAllow = false;
            
            if(fullscreenAAllow && fullscreenARef.indexOf(fullscreenADomain) > -1 && !document.location.pathname.match(/(\/shop\/|login\.bml|create\.bml)/))
            {
                fullscreenAShow();
                var expires = new Date();
                expires.setTime(expires.getTime() + (1 * 5 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
                expires = '; expires=' + expires.toUTCString();
                document.cookie = [fullscreenAName, '=1', expires, '; path=/', '; domain=.', fullscreenADomain].join('');
            }
            
            // End Hide -->

                )(liverailads_insert);

            }
            function onLiveRailAdEnd() {
                document.getElementById('takeoverFrame').style.display = 'none';
            }

Историческое событие - наконец-то мне подарили долгожданный агрегат для записи собственных творений: http://www.zoom.co.jp/english/products/h4n/Ура, товарищи! А то я было уже голову сломала, как сделать запись, если MiniDisc записывает, но на компьютер запись не перегоняет, если ноутбук записывает, но с  таким качеством звука, что лучше бы он этого не делал вовсе, а телефон Nokia Е7 записывает и даже на компьютер перегоняет, но от этого ни жарко, ни холодно...О результатах экспериментов обязуюсь доложить немедленно.

 Soon very soon

Apr. 19th, 2007 @ 03:49 pm 



Well haven't been around for awhile... oh well anyhow going to Nice, next week, for 10 days and then flying to Amsterdam, Minneapolis and Phoenix... yoohoo...The sun, my jacuzzi, friends, parties, my HB, the landscapes, the heat...Am so happy!!!!But right now still in Paris till election day (1st run) which is this coming Sunday, still undecided ( 1st time ever been undecided) there are 12 candidates to choose from.-2 extreme far right (FN & MPF)-1 extreme right (UMP)-1 center (UDF)-1 Green Party (les verts)-1 Socialist Party (PS)-4 Communist Parties (3 trotskist-leninist parties) (PCF, LO, LCR, PT)-1 Hunter, fisherman (more a lobby than a party) (CPNT)-1 antiliberal peasant (has no party)= so there is 3 parties on the right and 7 left, one center, and one neitherI'm still hesitating between 3 candidates... (left wing of course)For those who are interested the latest polls 3 days before the elections gives the top 525% Sarkozy (UMP party) (right winged candidate that represent the right of the right)21% Royal   (Socialist Party) right of the left20%Bayrou   (UDF party) the middle center guy15% Le pen  (FN Party) the far right extremist5 % Besancenot (LCR party) Trotskist-Leninist Party far left partythe others are under 5% of vote intentions...this is the 1st run the 2 best candidates goes on the 2nd run (in 2 weeks)5 years ago it was Chirac (UMP) against Le Pen (FN)we'll see...Current Mood: amusedCurrent Music: Prodigy

Les Debuts Erasmus - Bilan Du Premier Mois


Mar. 3rd, 2008 at 6:35 PM



  end asset-header 

J'arrive pas a y croire.. Vendredi, ca fera un mois que je suis arrivée ici.. Le temps passe trop vite! Peut etre justement parceque 6 mois c'est pas si long que ca, finalement!Je dois dire que j'ai jamais trop le temps d'ecrire et de donner de nouvelles, je suis désolée.. Mon appart est sympa, ms c'est pas vraiment a coté de mes facs.. au moins j'ai la plage :D  Je vais essayer de repondre a tt le monde cette semaine !Après la semaine d'inté, on a vité emmenagés dans nos apparts et les cours ont repris... Je commence a me rendre compte de ce que tout le monde me disait, en erasmus t'as vraiment trop envie de secher tous les cours quoi. C'est pas tellement parceque t'as quelque chose de mieux a faire, mais c'est juste que ... les cours sont pourris ! ^^  Le seul qui est bien c'est anglais, mais elle donne des devoirs donc enfait bof..On sort souvent avec mon groupe d'amis, peut etre pas autant que certains anciens erasmus mais assez pour etre crevée en fin de semaine^^  C'est d'ailleurs trés tentant de sortir sans raison vu que l'alcool est tellement moins cher ici ! 2€50 vodka redbull ca le fait...Tous les mercredis il y a des soirées ERASMUS organisées a Canalejas. Un bar ou t'as open bar de 10 a 11 ! et puis ensuite Paraninfo, avec son triple happy hour... La folie! Surtout que ici les verres de rhum coca par exemple, c'est un verre rempli de rhum et la mini bouteille de coca a coté.. Un peu plus et t'as pas la place de rajouter le soft..Ceci explique pourquoi mercredi dernier, j'etais (assez) bourrée et que j'ai envoyé des textos en anglais a tt le monde :)  D'ailleurs le lendemain matin, vive la gueule de bois ! Je crois que j'en ai jamais connu d'aussi puissante ^^ Le melange vin, bierre, vodka redbull, rhum orange, ca tue ! XDAutrement, avec mes colocs ca se passe vachement bien (ouff!) .. Il y a juste une filles que j'arrive pas a trop a cerner mais bon.. Des fois on se fait des soirées colocs, on va au resto et on joue aux cartes ou alrs on fait des jeux a boire avant d'aller en boite. Faudrait que je prenne une photo de mes colocs ^^Enfin samedi dernier, on a commencé a "voyager" un peu et donc on est allés a Maspalomas ( dans le sud de l'ile ). Maspalomas est connues pour ses dunes de sable. C'etait vraiment magnifique, un peu comme si on etait dans le sahara mais avec l'ocean a coté.. D'ailleurs ceux qui viendront me voir auront droit d'y aller aussi :)Dommage que la plage nudiste soit assez près des dunes et qu'il ny ait que des vieux.. parceque au pire si c'etait des jeunes, on aurait pu a moitié se rincer l'oeil.. Tampis !   Par contre, on aurait préféré eviter de tomlber sur un couple assez "occupé" au milieu des dunes.. Ils auraient pu trouver plus intime comme endroit, parceque les dunes, c'est un peu un des premiers endroits touristiques de Gran Canaria ! :D   [ Encore Plus De Nouvelles Photos ]


Location:Las Palmas de Gran CanariaMood:  satisfiedMusic:Gloria Estefan - Con Los Años Que Me Quedan

Tags:

erasmus, fac, friends, las palmas

Semaine D'Integration


Feb. 24th, 2008 at 11:06 PM



  end asset-header 

Petit résumé journée par journée Dimanche 10 : Rdv a l'hotel avec les coordinateurs. Enfait ils ne st pas venus mais ca aura au moins servi a ce qu'on se rencontre entre erasmus :) Le soir, diner sur le Paseo de Las Canteras avec quelques erasmus qui st devenus mes amis maintenant lol Lundi 11: Visite du rectorat et du service des relations internationales Tout une presentation sur l'université. Rencontre avec les mentors qui nous servent a rien ^^. Aprem libre pour chercher un appart ou aller a la plage :) Mardi 12: Visite de la faculté des Sciences Humaines (Obelisco) et test de niveau d'espagnol. Rencontre avec les coordinateurs qui enfait ne connaissent qu'un des etudiants venant de la rochelle sur 4.. Donc pr l'instant, Floriant, Blandine et moi, on est un peu a la rue ^^ Et puis ils comprennent pas ce que c'est LEA -_- depuis le tmps kils recoivent des etudiants francais qd mm ! Test d'espagnol trés ennuyant avec 100 questions avec 5 secondes par reponse.. Mercredi 13: Journée multiaventure Canoé-Kayac, tir a l'arc, escalade,etc.. Mais temps pourri ce qui nous a obligé a rester a l'abri pdt 2 heures ! -_- Dans l'aprem, visite de mon appart, signaure de contrat (j'ai pas le droit de fumer des joints ^^ c'est stipulé ds le contrat !), achat de carte sim espagnole... Soirée a Canalejas, bar où tous les mercredi ils organisent des soirées erasmus, avec open bar de 10 a 11 et a partir de 1h, toutes les boissons st a un euro ! :D En plus de ca, a l'entrée ils te donnent un numero et dc tu dois retrouver la personne qui a le meme numero que toi et les deux gagnent un shooter.. Ms avec 400 personnes va trouver ta paire ! ^^ Rentrée a 3h avec mon rire de bourée.. TsssJeudi 14: Visite des villages du nord de l'ile et Soirée bienvenue Erasmus a Tafira Visite de la rhumerie de Arucas où on a pu gouter ts les rhums arrangés.. rhum chocolat, rhum banane.. Absolument exquis malgrés la gueule de bois de la veille :p Visite de Teror, ville ou la vierge serait apparue ds un arbre.. Enfin dejeuner offert par les responsables de la semaine d'inté ds un resto au bord de la mer, paella, mojo con patatas, helado, etc.. Sieste pendant l'aprem, puis a 23h, soirée en "boite". Ebtre guillemets, pk enfet ct a l'air libre ! On se les gèle un peu, mais bon.. Vendredi 15 : Journée sur le bateau Dejeuner avec sarah chez le chinois. Embarquement a Puerto Rico ds le sud de l'ile. Dans le bateau, open bar, jacuzzi, DJ et diner organisé. On a longé la coté sud de l'ile pdt 2h (où j'ai fait tomber mes nouvelles lunettes de soleil - 3eme paire ds l'ocean atlantique depuis 3 ans^^), puis arret pour pouvoir plonger dans l'ocean.. :) C'etait juste le reve ! Samedi 16: Journée recherche d'appart Et puis journée libre pour ceux qui ont deja un appart :) Demmenagement de mes valises vers l'appart, rencontre avec mes colocs. Retour a l'hotel pour la dernière nuit. Le soir, fete a la plage de Alcaravaneras avec les Erasmus ! Dimanche 17: Derniers moments à l'hotel Petit dejeuner avec les amis a l'hotel :) Depart de l'hotel a midi, je m'installe completement. L'apremidi, rdv avec le ptit groupe pour aller a la plage. Le soir, visite de l'appart de Sarah et Diego, puis sortie ds le bar El Bote avec tt le monde :) Ouff ! Voila, voila :)  C'etait vraiment magnifique... En espérant que ces 6 mois restent comme ca ! :D et que c'est pas trop long a lire ^^


Location:Las Palmas de Gran CanariaMood:  accomplishedMusic:Lifehouse - Everything

Tags:

erasmus, friends, las palmas, welcoming week

            if (!pageNum) var pageNum = Math.round(Math.random() * 10000000000);
            document.write('<SCR');
            document.write('IPT LANGUAGE="JavaScript" SRC="http://ad.doubleclick.net/adj/lj.servicepages/fullscreenadsbml;'
                + 'a=1;r=0;w=1;wg=2;wa=23;wc=ES;ra=23;rg=2;jid=15008413;kw=las;kw=palmas;kw=erasmus;kw=friends;c=jo;pt=jo;scn=yes;' + 'a=1;r=0;w=0;c=se;pt=se' + ';dcopt=ist;fs=1;sz=1x1,pos=r;tile=1;ord=' + pageNum + '?" TYPE="text/javascript">');
            document.write('</SCR');
            document.write('IPT>');
                // ********* CODE FINISH *********
            }
            
            
            var fullscreenAName = 'ljfsads_client',
                fullscreenACook = document.cookie.split(';'),
                fullscreenAAllow = true,
                fullscreenADomain = Site.siteroot,
                fullscreenARef = document.referrer;
            
            fullscreenADomain = fullscreenADomain.split('.');
            fullscreenADomain.shift();
            fullscreenADomain = fullscreenADomain.join('.');
            
            for(var i = 0, l = fullscreenACook.length; i < l; i++) if(fullscreenACook[i].indexOf(fullscreenAName) > -1) fullscreenAAllow = false;
            
            if(fullscreenAAllow && fullscreenARef.indexOf(fullscreenADomain) > -1 && !document.location.pathname.match(/(\/shop\/|login\.bml|create\.bml)/))
            {
                fullscreenAShow();
                var expires = new Date();
                expires.setTime(expires.getTime() + (1 * 5 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
                expires = '; expires=' + expires.toUTCString();
                document.cookie = [fullscreenAName, '=1', expires, '; path=/', '; domain=.', fullscreenADomain].join('');
            }
            
            // End Hide -->
